<div class="icbu-mod-wrapper no-title module-customArea no-bg-color"><div class="wrap-box"><div class="mod-content"><div class="custom-content"><p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">buononaturale addresses our need for a&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><strong>safe and sustainable lifestyle</strong></span>&nbsp;by piecing together stories from&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><strong>Italy&rsquo;s ancient agricultural and zootechnical traditions</strong></span>, starting from the vast province of Irpinia that flanks the Italian Apennines, among the oldest mountain ranges in Europe. In collaboration with a multitude of&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><strong>micro-to-small-sized farms</strong>&nbsp;</span>and the human stories that back them, we work on making sure that as many people as possible have access to our&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><strong>natural local Italian specialties</strong></span>, either directly or through our distributors located across the globe.</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-size:18px;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">At every bite, our products will take you through the most scenic Italian landscapes, from the Apennine farmlands to the rice fields of the Po valley, which they originate from and whose smells and flavors they still retain. We ensure that our products reflect their &ldquo;high quality&rdquo; label in light of both the&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><strong>traditional artisanal processes</strong>&nbsp;</span>and the&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><strong>best-in-class ingredients</strong>&nbsp;</span>employed to obtain them. Our sourcing and production choices are meant to realize the widespread desire for a diet that is <em>healthy</em>, <em>sustainable</em>, and <em>inspired</em> by the lively colors and dense flavors of rural life, and specifically of the <em>wholesome Italian rural life</em>.</span></p></div></div></div></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="icbu-mod-wrapper no-title module-customArea no-bg-color"><div class="wrap-box"><div class="mod-content"><div class="custom-content"><p>&nbsp;</p>
<table style="width:765px;border:solid 5px #206B05;" border="5" data-mce-background-color="#nannannan">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center;width:176px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;"><strong>Preserved Vegetables</strong>: <em>ORGANIC</em>, <em>VEGAN OK</em>, <em>FREE FROM</em></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">Ranging from <span style="color:#339966;"><em>dried tomatoes</em> </span>to <span style="color:#339966;"><em>artichokes</em> </span>and <span style="color:#339966;"><em>capers</em></span>, our preserves serve many purposes. They are ideal for preparing salads as much as intricate pasta dishes, or you can simply serve them as elegant finger food for your happy hours with friends and family.&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>Legumes</em> </span>are among our favorite preserves, and we offer them boiled.</span></p>
</td>
<td style="text-align:center;width:205px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;"><strong>Sauces and Condiments</strong>: <em>ORGANIC</em>, (also) <em>VEGAN OK</em> and <em>GLUTEN FREE</em>,&nbsp;<em>FREE FROM</em></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">Our&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>ready-to-use&nbsp;</em></span>sauces and condiments&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>reformulate</em>&nbsp;</span>traditional Italian recipes in a vegan, plant-based, or gluten-free fashion: so, our Ligurian pestoghiotto is also available as Vegetable pestoghiotto, our mayonnaise as Soy-based mayonnaise, and Bolognese rag&ugrave; as Seitan- or Soy-based tomato sauce.</span></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align:center;width:176px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<div class="term-description">
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;"><strong>Rice</strong>:&nbsp;<em>ORGANIC</em></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">Our organic rice is available in three formats &ndash; 500g, 1kg, and 5kg &ndash; and as one of four 100% Italian organic and all-natural varieties: two risotto-making varieties,&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>Arborio</em>&nbsp;</span>and&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>Carnaroli</em></span>, and two wholegrain ones that are easy to digest and rich in nutritional properties,&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>red wild</em>&nbsp;</span>and&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>black Nerone</em></span>.</span></p>
</div>
</td>
<td style="text-align:center;width:205px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<div class="term-description">
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;"><strong>Ready-To-Cook Meals</strong>:&nbsp;<em>ORGANIC</em>,&nbsp;<em>VEGAN OK</em></span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p><span style="font-size:18px;font-family:georgia,palatino;">Our organic&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>ready-to-cook&nbsp;</em></span>range includes risotto, polenta, spelt, and barley meals. They derive from the combination of&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>pre-cooked</em>&nbsp;</span>rice, semolina, or ancient cereals with&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>dehydrated vegetables</em></span>, according to our original broth recipe that preserves the typical properties of these homemade dishes. Set aside 5 to 17 minutes, a pot of boiling water, and a ladle to serve this &ldquo;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>meal for three</em></span>&rdquo; with little effort.</span></p>
</div>
</td>

<tr>
<td style="width:225.513px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<div class="term-description">
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;"><strong>Truffle Specialties</strong>:&nbsp;<em>TRADITIONAL</em></span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">Truffle is a mysterious ingredient of Italy&rsquo;s gastronomic tradition, known for its penetrating smell and aphrodisiac properties. Our truffles are available as&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>carpaccios</em></span>&nbsp;with olive oil,&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>aromatized extra-virgin olive oils</em></span>, or&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>sauces</em>&nbsp;</span>to color your meals.</span></p>
</div>
</td>
<td style="width:137.487px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<div class="term-description">
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;"><strong>Pasta</strong>:&nbsp;<em>TRADITIONAL</em>,&nbsp;<em>PREMIUM</em></span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">Our pasta, whether dried, fresh, or frozen, is made with&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>water from our mountains</em></span>,&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>flour from our farms</em></span>, and&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>stuffing ingredients from our soils</em></span>. Our dried pasta is artisanally&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>bronze wire-drawn</em>&nbsp;</span>and&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>slowly dried</em>&nbsp;</span>for 40 hours at low temperature in order to preserve all the aromas of the grain.</span></p>
</div>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="width:225.513px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<div class="term-description">
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;"><strong>Spreadable Creams</strong>:&nbsp;<em>TRADITIONAL</em></span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">Our creams are made from 30% of premium dried fruit:&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>pistachio</em></span>,&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>almond</em></span>, or&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>hazelnut</em></span>.&nbsp;These can be eaten in spoonfuls, spread over bread, or used to fill sweets and panettoni.&nbsp;Such a&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>high concentration&nbsp;</em></span>of the primary ingredient in our creams allows for significant dilution to make delicious chantilly creams.</span></p>
</div>
</td>
<td style="width:137.487px;border:5px solid #206B05;">
<div class="term-description">
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span class="font" style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;"><strong>Sauces and Condiments</strong>:&nbsp;<em>TRADITIONAL</em></span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-align:center;"><span class="font" style="font-family:georgia,palatino;font-size:18px;">Our&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>dried fruit pestos&nbsp;</em></span>contain 60% of premium dried fruits from Sicily. The pestos are meant to be used as&nbsp;<span style="color:#339966;"><em>savory sauces</em></span>, containing dried fruit grains that stick to the heterogenous surfaces of pasta shapes such as Fusilli, Penne rigate, and others.</span></p>
</div>
</td>

<script>
    // 买家收藏夹 html espace twice bug fixed
    if(window.location.pathname === '/favorite2/favorite_home.htm' && typeof MutationObserver === 'function') {

        function observeTarget(rootSelector, modifySelector) {
            var $root = document.querySelector(rootSelector)
            var isFirst = true
            var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutationsList) {
                function doReplace() {
                    var nList = document.querySelectorAll(modifySelector)
                    var nListArr = Array.prototype.slice.call(nList, null)
                    nListArr.forEach(function($nodeItem) {
                        $nodeItem.innerHTML = $nodeItem.innerText
                    })
                }
                
                if(isFirst) {
                    setTimeout(doReplace, 2000)
                    isFirst = false
                } else {
                    doReplace()
                }
            })
            
            observer.observe($root, { attributes: true, childList: false, subtree: false })
        }

        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            var rootSelector = '.fav-list-box.product-list-box'
            var modifySelector = '.suppliers-list-box .item-suppliers-name'
            
            observeTarget(rootSelector, modifySelector)
        })

    }
</script>

            link.type='text/css';
            link.rel = 'stylesheet';
            link.href = url;
            head.appendChild(link);
        })("//s.alicdn.com/@g/sc/services-module/1.0.14/sc-services-module/index.css");

          if (str) {
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.type = 'text/javascript';

            script.defer = true;

      }

<script>
    try{
        var loadScript = function (url, callback) {
          var script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = url;
          script.async = true;
          if (script.addEventListener) {
            script.addEventListener('load', function () {
              callback();
            }, false);
          } else if (script.attachEvent) {
            script.attachEvent('onreadystatechange', function () {
              var target = window.event.srcElement;
              if (target.readyState === 'loaded') {
                callback();
              }
            });
          }
          document.body.appendChild(script);
        };
        
        var loadCss = function (url) {
          var style = document.createElement('link');
          style.rel = 'stylesheet';
          style.href = url;
          document.head.appendChild(style);
        }

        window.BzEvaluate = {};
        window.BzEvaluate.loadSurvey = function (params) {
          loadScript('https://air.alibaba.com/app/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/pages_version.html', function () {
            // 加载css
            loadCss('https://s.alicdn.com/@g/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/' + window._BZ_VERSION_.version + '/pages/survey/index.web.css', 'css');
            // 加载js
            loadScript('https://s.alicdn.com/@g/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/'+ window._BZ_VERSION_.version + '/pages/survey/index.web.js', function () {
              // 执行页面渲染
              window.BzEvaluate.render(params);
            });
          });
        }
        
        var bz_survey_config_scene = "";
        
        if(location.href.indexOf('profile.alibaba.com/profile/buyer_selection.htm') > -1){
            // 买家选品
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'ma_buyer_selection_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (/^https:\/\/www.alibaba.com\/trueview\/.*(_\d+.html)$/.test(location.href)) {
            // true view 沉浸页
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'true_view_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (location.href.indexOf('www.alibaba.com/trade/search') > -1) {
            // 搜索页
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'search_list_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (location.hostname == 'www.alibaba.com' && location.pathname === '/') {
            // 首页
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'buyer_pc_home_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (location.href.indexOf('www.alibaba.com/live/') > -1 || location.href.indexOf('watch.alibaba.com/v/') > -1 ) {
            // 直播
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'live_room_questionnaire_location';
        } else if (/^https:\/\/i\.alibaba\.com\/globalBuyerIndex\.htm/.test(location.href)) {
            bz_survey_config_scene = 'buyer_pc_ma_questionnaire_location';
        }
         
        
        if(bz_survey_config_scene){
                                    
            window.BzEvaluate.loadSurvey({
              type: 'dialog',
              link: 'https://air.alibaba.com/app/sc-assets/bz-evaluate/pages_survey.html?bizCode=' + bz_survey_config_scene + '&status=none&targetType=BUYER',
              style: {
                bottom: '100px',
                right: 0,  
              },
              callback: function () {}
            });
        }
    }catch(e){
        
    }
</script>
